Garuda-Purana
Part 3

Based on the edition Bombay : Venkatesvara Steam Press (or a reprint thereof)


Input by members of the SANSKNET-project
(www.sansknet.org)



This GRETIL version has been converted from a custom Devanagari encoding.
Consequently, many word boundaries are not marked by spaces.
The Nagari e-text follows the layout and graphic appearance of the printed 
edition very closely. It even adds blanks when a line break cuts through 
a word or compound.
These and other irregularities cannot be standardized at present.

After many corrections, the text is in need of further proof reading!

÷rãgaruóamahàpuràõam- 2
÷rã÷aunaka uvàca  /
kathaü sasarja bhagavàüstattattattvàbhimàninaş  /
sçùñikramaü na jànàmi devànàü hyantaraü mune  // GarP_3,2.1 //
÷aunakenaiva muktastu såto vacanamabravãt  /
÷åta uvàca  /
samyagvyavasità buddhistava brahmarùisattama  // GarP_3,2.2 //
evameva kçtaş pra÷ro harau tu garuóena vai  /
yaduktavànharistasmaitadvakùyàmi tavànagha  /
